| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox CSS Style Resolution to Layout Paint Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the style change notification, the frame style recomputation, the dirty-frame reflow scheduling, the display list construction, and the WebRender layer update.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

532026-03-08T20:36:41.852373agentmessage-
I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the CSS style change → layout → paint chain in Firefox/Gecko. Let me summarize the key files and functions:

## The Chain

### 1. Style Change Notification
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** - `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()` - Entry point for style change notifications. Calls `Servo_NoteExplicitHints()` to mark elements dirty.
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.h`** - Header for RestyleManager
- **`layout/style/nsChangeHint.h`** - Defines change hint flags (nsChangeHint_NeedReflow, nsChangeHint_RepaintFrame, etc.)

### 2. Style Traversal (Servo/Stylo)
- **`layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp`** - `ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument()` - Performs the Servo style traversal using `Servo_TraverseSubtree()`. This is the actual style computation.
- **`layout/style/ServoStyleSet.h`** - Header
- **`servo/components/style/traversal.rs`** - Rust-side style traversal

### 3. Frame Style Recomputation (Post-Traversal)
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** - `RestyleManager::DoProcessPendingRestyles()` - Orchestrates the full restyle process
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** - `RestyleManager::ProcessPostTraversal()` - Processes each element after style traversal, collects change hints
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** - `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()` - Processes the change hints list
- **`layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp`** - `nsIFrame::DidSetComputedStyle()` - Called when a frame's computed style changes

### 4. Dirty-Frame Reflow Scheduling

Here is the complete, precise trace of the **CSS style change → layout → paint chain** in Firefox/Gecko (mozilla/gecko-dev), with every key C++ source file and function identified from the actual source.

---

## The Full Pipeline

```
CSS property change
      │
      ▼  [1] Style Change Notification
RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()
      │  Servo_NoteExplicitHints()  ← marks element dirty in Servo
      ▼  [2] Style Traversal (Servo/Stylo)
ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument()
      │  Servo_TraverseSubtree()    ← Rust-side parallel style computation
      ▼  [3] Post-Traversal / Frame Style Recomputation
RestyleManager::ProcessPostTraversal()
      │  nsIFrame::DidSetComputedStyle()
      │  → collects nsChangeHint flags
      ▼  [4] Change Hint Dispatch
RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()
      ├──[reflow hints]──► StyleChangeReflow()
      │                        └─► PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()  ← dirty bits + mDirtyRoots
      └──[paint hints]───► ApplyRenderingChangeToTree()
                               └─► nsIFrame::SchedulePaint()
                                       └─► PresShell::SchedulePaint()
      ▼  [5] Display List Construction
nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame()
      │  nsDisplayListBuilder (created)
      │  nsIFrame::BuildDisplayList()  ← virtual, per frame type
      ▼  [6] WebRender Layer Update
WebRenderCommandBuilder::BuildWebRenderCommands()
      │  CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList()
      ▼
WebRenderLayerManager::EndTransactionWithoutLayer()
      │  wr::DisplayListBuilder::End()
      ▼
WebRenderBridgeChild::EndTransaction()
      │  SendSetDisplayList()  ← IPC to GPU/compositor process
      ▼
  WebRender compositor renders frame
```
